    Type: AWS::EC2::Volume
    Properties:
      AvailabilityZone: !Sub '${AWS::Region}a'
      Size: 1000
      VolumeType: st1
      Encrypted: true
      KmsKeyId: !Ref EBSEncryptionKey
      Tags:
        - Key: Name
          Value: !Sub 'anihpj-analytics-${Environment}'
        - Key: Environment
          Value: !Ref Environment
        - Key: Application
          Value: anihpj-jobpost
        - Key: Purpose
          Value: big-data-processing

Outputs:
  DatabaseVolumeId:
    Description: ID of the database EBS volume
    Value: !Ref DatabaseVolume
    Export:
      Name: !Sub '${AWS::StackName}-DatabaseVolumeId'
  
  WebServerVolume1Id:
    Description: ID of web server 1 EBS volume
    Value: !Ref WebServerVolume1
    Export:
      Name: !Sub '${AWS::StackName}-WebServerVolume1Id'
  
  WebServerVolume2Id:
    Description: ID of web server 2 EBS volume  
    Value: !Ref WebServerVolume2
    Export:
      Name: !Sub '${AWS::StackName}-WebServerVolume2Id'
  
  AnalyticsVolumeId:
    Description: ID of analytics EBS volume
    Value: !Ref AnalyticsVolume
    Export:
      Name: !Sub '${AWS::StackName}-AnalyticsVolumeId'
  
  KMSKeyId:
    Description: KMS Key ID for EBS encryption
    Value: !Ref EBSEncryptionKey
    Export:
      Name: !Sub '${AWS::StackName}-KMSKeyId'
🔄 CI/CD Pipeline Integration
📝 GitHub Actions Workflow for EBS Management
# .github/workflows/ebs-management.yml
name: anihpj EBS Management

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
    paths: ['infrastructure/ebs/**']
  schedule:
    - cron: '0 2 * * *'  # Daily backup at 2 AM
  workflow_dispatch:
    inputs:
      action:
        description: 'Action to perform'
        required: true
        default: 'backup'
        type: choice
        options:
          - backup
          - cleanup
          - resize

env:
  AWS_REGION: us-east-1
  ENVIRONMENT: production

jobs:
  ebs-backup:
    if: github.event_name == 'schedule' || (github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' && github.event.inputs.action == 'backup')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      id-token: write
      contents: read
    
    steps:
      - name: Checkout code
        uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Configure AWS credentials
        uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v4
        with:
          role-to-assume: ${{ secrets.AWS_ROLE_ARN }}
          role-session-name: anihpj-ebs-backup
          aws-region: ${{ env.AWS_REGION }}
      
      - name: Setup Python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v4
        with:
          python-version: '3.9'
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: |
          pip install boto3 click
      
      - name: Create EBS snapshots
        run: |
          python scripts/ebs_backup.py \
            --environment ${{ env.ENVIRONMENT }} \
            --application anihpj-jobpost \
            --retention-days 7
      
      - name: Notify on failure
        if: failure()
        uses: 8398a7/action-slack@v3
        with:
          status: failure
          text: 'anihpj EBS backup failed!'
        env:
          SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL: ${{ secrets.SLACK_WEBHOOK }}

  ebs-resize:
    if: github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' && github.event.inputs.action == 'resize'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: production
    
    steps:
      - name: Checkout code
        uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
      - name: Configure AWS credentials
        uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v4
        with:
          role-to-assume: ${{ secrets.AWS_ROLE_ARN }}
          aws-region: ${{ env.AWS_REGION }}
      
      - name: Check volume utilization
        id: check_utilization
        run: |
          python scripts/check_volume_usage.py \
            --threshold 80 \
            --output-format github-actions
      
      - name: Resize volumes if needed
        if: steps.check_utilization.outputs.resize_needed == 'true'
        run: |
          python scripts/resize_volumes.py \
            --dry-run false \
            --increase-percentage 20
      
      - name: Update Terraform state
        if: steps.check_utilization.outputs.resize_needed == 'true'
        run: |
          terraform init
          terraform refresh
          terraform plan -out=tfplan
          terraform apply tfplan
🤖 Automated Backup Pipeline
📝 Complete Backup Automation Script
# scripts/ebs_backup.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
anihpj EBS Backup Automation Script
Handles creating, managing, and cleaning up EBS snapshots
"""

import boto3
import click
import json
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import List, Dict

# Configure logging
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class EBSBackupManager:
    def __init__(self, region: str = 'us-east-1'):
        self.ec2 = boto3.client('ec2', region_name=region)
        self.region = region
    
    def get_volumes_to_backup(self, application: str, environment: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """Get all volumes that need backup based on tags"""
        try:
            response = self.ec2.describe_volumes(
                Filters=[
                    {'Name': 'tag:Application', 'Values': [application]},
                    {'Name': 'tag:Environment', 'Values': [environment]},
                    {'Name': 'tag:BackupSchedule', 'Values': ['daily', 'weekly']},
                    {'Name': 'state', 'Values': ['in-use', 'available']}
                ]
            )
            return response['Volumes']
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error retrieving volumes: {e}")
            return []
    
    def create_snapshot(self, volume: Dict, retention_days: int = 7) -> str:
        """Create snapshot for a volume"""
        volume_id = volume['VolumeId']
        
        # Extract volume name from tags
        volume_name = next(
            (tag['Value'] for tag in volume['Tags'] if tag['Key'] == 'Name'),
            volume_id
        )
        
        # Extract backup schedule
        backup_schedule = next(
            (tag['Value'] for tag in volume['Tags'] if tag['Key'] == 'BackupSchedule'),
            'daily'
        )
        
        description = f"Automated {backup_schedule} backup of {volume_name} - {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}"
        
        try:
            response = self.ec2.create_snapshot(
                VolumeId=volume_id,
                Description=description,
                TagSpecifications=[{
                    'ResourceType': 'snapshot',
                    'Tags': [
                        {'Key': 'Name', 'Value': f"{volume_name}-{backup_schedule}-{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')}"},
                        {'Key': 'Application', 'Value': 'anihpj-jobpost'},
                        {'Key': 'CreatedBy', 'Value': 'EBS-Backup-Automation'},
                        {'Key': 'BackupType', 'Value': backup_schedule},
                        {'Key': 'RetentionDays', 'Value': str(retention_days)},
                        {'Key': 'SourceVolume', 'Value': volume_id},
                        {'Key': 'CreatedDate', 'Value': datetime.now().isoformat()}
                    ]
                }]
            )
            
            snapshot_id = response['SnapshotId']
            logger.info(f"Created snapshot {snapshot_id} for volume {volume_id}")
            return snapshot_id
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error creating snapshot for volume {volume_id}: {e}")
            return None
    
    def cleanup_old_snapshots(self, retention_days: int = 7, application: str = 'anihpj-jobpost'):
        """Remove snapshots older than retention period"""
        cutoff_date = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=retention_days)
        
        try:
            response = self.ec2.describe_snapshots(
                OwnerIds=['self'],
                Filters=[
                    {'Name': 'tag:Application', 'Values': [application]},
                    {'Name': 'tag:CreatedBy', 'Values': ['EBS-Backup-Automation']}
                ]
            )
            
            deleted_count = 0
            for snapshot in response['Snapshots']:
                # Check retention days from tags
                retention_tag = next(
                    (tag['Value'] for tag in snapshot.get('Tags', []) if tag['Key'] == 'RetentionDays'),
                    str(retention_days)
                )
                
                snapshot_retention = int(retention_tag)
                snapshot_cutoff = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=snapshot_retention)
                
                if snapshot['StartTime'].replace(tzinfo=None) < snapshot_cutoff:
                    try:
                        self.ec2.delete_snapshot(SnapshotId=snapshot['SnapshotId'])
                        logger.info(f"Deleted old snapshot: {snapshot['SnapshotId']}")
                        deleted_count += 1
                    except Exception as e:
                        logger.error(f"Error deleting snapshot {snapshot['SnapshotId']}: {e}")
            
            logger.info(f"Cleaned up {deleted_count} old snapshots")
            return deleted_count
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error during cleanup: {e}")
            return 0

@click.command()
@click.option('--environment', '-e', default='production', help='Environment name')
@click.option('--application', '-a', default='anihpj-jobpost', help='Application name')
@click.option('--retention-days', '-r', default=7, help='Snapshot retention in days')
@click.option('--cleanup-only', is_flag=True, help='Only perform cleanup, skip backup')
@click.option('--region', default='us-east-1', help='AWS region')
def main(environment, application, retention_days, cleanup_only, region):
    """anihpj EBS Backup Automation"""
    
    backup_manager = EBSBackupManager(region)
    
    if not cleanup_only:
        # Create new snapshots
        volumes = backup_manager.get_volumes_to_backup(application, environment)
        logger.info(f"Found {len(volumes)} volumes to backup")
        
        created_snapshots = []
        for volume in volumes:
            snapshot_id = backup_manager.create_snapshot(volume, retention_days)
            if snapshot_id:
                created_snapshots.append(snapshot_id)
        
        logger.info(f"Successfully created {len(created_snapshots)} snapshots")
    
    # Cleanup old snapshots
    deleted_count = backup_manager.cleanup_old_snapshots(retention_days, application)
    
    # Output results for CI/CD integration
    results = {
        'status': 'success',
        'snapshots_created': len(created_snapshots) if not cleanup_only else 0,
        'snapshots_deleted': deleted_count,
        'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
    }
    
    print(json.dumps(results, indent=2))

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

📊 Audit & Monitoring
📝 CloudWatch Compliance Dashboard
# compliance_monitoring.py
import boto3
import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class EBSComplianceMonitor:
    def __init__(self, region='us-east-1'):
        self.ec2 = boto3.client('ec2', region_name=region)
        self.config = boto3.client('config', region_name=region)
        self.cloudwatch = boto3.client('cloudwatch', region_name=region)
    
    def check_encryption_compliance(self):
        """Check if all EBS volumes are encrypted"""
        volumes = self.ec2.describe_volumes()
        
        total_volumes = len(volumes['Volumes'])
        encrypted_volumes = sum(1 for vol in volumes['Volumes'] if vol.get('Encrypted', False))
        
        compliance_percentage = (encrypted_volumes / total_volumes) * 100 if total_volumes > 0 else 100
        
        # Send metric to CloudWatch
        self.cloudwatch.put_metric_data(
            Namespace='anihpj/EBS/Compliance',
            MetricData=[
                {
                    'MetricName': 'EncryptionCompliance',
                    'Value': compliance_percentage,
                    'Unit': 'Percent',
                    'Dimensions': [
                        {
                            'Name': 'Application',
                            'Value': 'anihpj-jobpost'
                        }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        )
        
        return {
            'total_volumes': total_volumes,
            'encrypted_volumes': encrypted_volumes,
            'compliance_percentage': compliance_percentage
        }
    
    def check_backup_compliance(self):
        """Check if volumes have recent backups"""
        volumes = self.ec2.describe_volumes(
            Filters=[{
                'Name': 'tag:Application',
                'Values': ['anihpj-jobpost']
            }]
        )
        
        compliant_volumes = 0
        total_volumes = len(volumes['Volumes'])
        
        for volume in volumes['Volumes']:
            volume_id = volume['VolumeId']
            
            # Check for recent snapshots (within 24 hours)
            snapshots = self.ec2.describe_snapshots(
                OwnerIds=['self'],
                Filters=[
                    {'Name': 'volume-id', 'Values': [volume_id]},
                    {'Name': 'status', 'Values': ['completed']}
                ]
            )
            
            recent_snapshots = [
                s for s in snapshots['Snapshots']
                if s['StartTime'] > datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)
            ]
            
            if recent_snapshots:
                compliant_volumes += 1
        
        compliance_percentage = (compliant_volumes / total_volumes) * 100 if total_volumes > 0 else 100
        
        # Send metric to CloudWatch
        self.cloudwatch.put_metric_data(
            Namespace='anihpj/EBS/Compliance',
            MetricData=[
                {
                    'MetricName': 'BackupCompliance',
                    'Value': compliance_percentage,
                    'Unit': 'Percent'
                }
            ]
        )
        
        return {
            'total_volumes': total_volumes,
            'compliant_volumes': compliant_volumes,
            'compliance_percentage': compliance_percentage
        }
    
    def generate_compliance_report(self):
        """Generate comprehensive compliance report"""
        encryption_status = self.check_encryption_compliance()
        backup_status = self.check_backup_compliance()
        
        report = {
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'application': 'anihpj-jobpost',
            'encryption_compliance': encryption_status,
            'backup_compliance': backup_status,
            'overall_score': (
                encryption_status['compliance_percentage'] + 
                backup_status['compliance_percentage']
            ) / 2
        }
        
        return report

# Usage
if __name__ == "__main__":
    monitor = EBSComplianceMonitor()
    report = monitor.generate_compliance_report()
    print(json.dumps(report, indent=2))

📝 Glossary

📦 Availability Zone (AZ)

Isolated locations within AWS regions. EBS volumes can only be attached to EC2 instances in the same AZ.

🔄 Block Storage

Raw storage that can be mounted to an operating system and formatted with a file system. EBS provides block-level storage.

📸 EBS Snapshot

Point-in-time backup of EBS volumes stored in Amazon S3. Used for backup, recovery, and creating new volumes.

🔒 EBS Encryption

Feature that encrypts EBS volumes using AWS KMS keys, providing data protection at rest and in transit to storage.

⚡ EBS-Optimized Instance

EC2 instances with dedicated bandwidth for EBS traffic, ensuring consistent performance between compute and storage.

🔧 Elastic Volumes

Feature allowing dynamic modification of volume size, performance (IOPS), and volume type without stopping instances.

⚡ Fast Snapshot Restore (FSR)

Feature that enables immediate full performance when creating volumes from snapshots, eliminating initialization penalty.

📊 IOPS (Input/Output Operations Per Second)

Measurement of storage performance. EBS offers different IOPS capabilities across volume types (gp3: 3,000-16,000, io2: up to 64,000).

🔑 KMS (Key Management Service)

AWS service for creating and managing encryption keys used for EBS volume encryption and other AWS services.

⏱️ Latency

Time delay between request and response. EBS provides low-latency storage for EC2 instances, typically sub-millisecond.

🔄 Multi-Attach

EBS feature allowing a single io1 or io2 volume to be attached to multiple EC2 instances simultaneously in same AZ.

🏗️ Provisioned IOPS

Storage option (io1, io2) that allows specification of exact IOPS requirements, up to 64,000 IOPS per volume.

📈 Queue Depth

Number of pending I/O requests to a storage device. Higher queue depths can improve IOPS utilization on EBS volumes.

🛠️ Root Volume

EBS volume containing the operating system. Can be configured to persist after instance termination (delete-on-termination = false).

📊 Throughput

Amount of data transferred per second. EBS gp3 volumes support up to 1,000 MiB/s, while other types vary by size and type.

🗂️ Volume Type

EBS storage categories optimized for different use cases:

  • gp3: General Purpose SSD (latest generation)
  • gp2: General Purpose SSD (previous generation)
  • io2: Provisioned IOPS SSD (latest generation)
  • io1: Provisioned IOPS SSD (previous generation)
  • st1: Throughput Optimized HDD
  • sc1: Cold HDD

🎯 anihpj-Specific Terms

anihpj Job Portal: Django-based web application for job postings and applications, used as reference architecture throughout this documentation.

Database Volume: High-performance EBS volume (typically io2) dedicated to PostgreSQL database storage for anihpj application.

Media Volume: General-purpose EBS volume (typically gp3) for storing user uploads, resumes, and static content.

Analytics Volume: Cost-optimized EBS volume (typically st1) for big data processing and job market analytics.

🔄 Migration Scenarios
📈 From On-Premises to EBS
📍 Before (On-Premises)
  • Physical storage arrays
  • Manual provisioning (weeks)
  • Fixed capacity planning
  • Hardware maintenance overhead
  • Single point of failure
☁️ After (Amazon EBS)
  • Elastic cloud storage
  • Instant provisioning (minutes)
  • Dynamic scaling
  • AWS-managed infrastructure
  • Built-in redundancy
🔧 gp2 to gp3 Migration Benefits
# Migration script for anihpj volumes
#!/bin/bash

# List current gp2 volumes
aws ec2 describe-volumes \
    --filters "Name=volume-type,Values=gp2" "Name=tag:Application,Values=anihpj-jobpost" \
    --query 'Volumes[*].[VolumeId,Size,Tags[?Key==`Name`].Value|[0]]' \
    --output table

# Modify volumes to gp3 (20% cost reduction, better performance)
for volume_id in $(aws ec2 describe-volumes \
    --filters "Name=volume-type,Values=gp2" "Name=tag:Application,Values=anihpj-jobpost" \
    --query 'Volumes[*].VolumeId' --output text); do
    
    echo "Migrating volume $volume_id from gp2 to gp3..."
    
    aws ec2 modify-volume \
        --volume-id $volume_id \
        --volume-type gp3 \
        --iops 3000 \
        --throughput 125
    
    echo "Migration initiated for $volume_id"
done

# Estimated savings for anihpj:
# 500GB gp2: $50/month → gp3: $40/month (20% savings)
# 1TB gp2: $100/month → gp3: $80/month (20% savings)
🎯 Decision Matrix for anihpj
Scenario Recommended Volume Size Reasoning Monthly Cost
Production PostgreSQL io2 500GB, 10,000 IOPS High consistency, low latency required ~$712/month
Development Database gp3 100GB, 3,000 IOPS Cost-effective, adequate performance ~$8/month
Web Server Storage gp3 50GB, 3,000 IOPS General purpose, Django application ~$4/month
Analytics Processing st1 2TB High throughput for big data ~$90/month
Log Archive sc1 5TB Infrequent access, cost optimization ~$75/month
Backup Storage S3 (not EBS) 1TB snapshots Long-term retention, cross-region ~$23/month
